### [105] [Dynamics-Informed Deep Learning for Predicting Extreme Events](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.10777)
*Eirini Katsidoniotaki,Themistoklis P. Sapsis*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了一个纯数据驱动的框架，通过构建基于有限时间李雅普诺夫指数（FTLE）类前兆信号来预测高维混沌系统中的极端事件，无需已知控制方程即可识别导致极端事件的瞬态不稳定机制，显著延长了预测时效。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 高维混沌动力系统中极端事件的预测是一个根本性挑战。这类事件具有稀有性、间歇性特征，且由难以从有限观测中推断的瞬态动力学机制驱动。传统方法依赖统计关联，无法捕捉驱动极端事件的潜在机制，难以实现实时长时效预测。

Method: 提出一个完全数据驱动的框架：1）利用降阶公式直接从状态快照计算FTLE类前兆信号，无需已知控制方程；2）为避免经典FTLE计算的高昂成本，在由最优时间依赖（OTD）模式张成的自适应演化低维子空间中评估不稳定增长，高效识别瞬态放大方向；3）将这些机制感知的前兆信号输入基于Transformer的模型，预测极端事件的可观测量。

Result: 在Kolmogorov流（间歇性湍流的典型模型）上验证了该框架。结果表明，与基于可观测量输入的基线方法相比，显式编码瞬态不稳定机制能够显著延长实用的预测时间范围。

Conclusion: 通过显式追踪极端事件发生前的瞬态不稳定性并构建可解释的、机制感知的前兆信号，可以有效延长高维混沌系统中极端事件的预测时效。该方法为无需已知控制方程的数据驱动极端事件预测提供了新途径。

Abstract: Predicting extreme events in high-dimensional chaotic dynamical systems remains a fundamental challenge, as such events are rare, intermittent, and arise from transient dynamical mechanisms that are difficult to infer from limited observations. Accordingly, real-time forecasting calls for precursors that encode the mechanisms driving extremes, rather than relying solely on statistical associations. We propose a fully data-driven framework for long-lead prediction of extreme events that constructs interpretable, mechanism-aware precursors by explicitly tracking transient instabilities preceding event onset. The approach leverages a reduced-order formulation to compute finite-time Lyapunov exponent (FTLE)-like precursors directly from state snapshots, without requiring knowledge of the governing equations. To avoid the prohibitive computational cost of classical FTLE computation, instability growth is evaluated in an adaptively evolving low-dimensional subspace spanned by Optimal Time-Dependent (OTD) modes, enabling efficient identification of transiently amplifying directions. These precursors are then provided as input to a Transformer-based model, enabling forecast of extreme event observables. We demonstrate the framework on Kolmogorov flow, a canonical model of intermittent turbulence. The results show that explicitly encoding transient instability mechanisms substantially extends practical prediction horizons compared to baseline observable-based approaches.

Motivation: 轨迹预测对自动驾驶的安全与效率至关重要，但最先进的预测模型对轻微的对抗性扰动攻击非常脆弱，而目前针对此类攻击的有效防御手段研究有限。

Result: 该方法能够在多个数据集上持续提升多种基础轨迹预测模型的预测鲁棒性，且在非对抗性设置下不牺牲预测精度，具有简单且计算成本低的优势。

Conclusion: 随机平滑是一种简单、计算成本低且有效的技术，可用于缓解轨迹预测中的对抗攻击问题。

Abstract: Accurate and robust trajectory prediction is essential for safe and efficient autonomous driving, yet recent work has shown that even state-of-the-art prediction models are highly vulnerable to inputs being mildly perturbed by adversarial attacks. Although model vulnerabilities to such attacks have been studied, work on effective countermeasures remains limited. In this work, we develop and evaluate a new defense mechanism for trajectory prediction models based on randomized smoothing -- an approach previously applied successfully in other domains. We evaluate its ability to improve model robustness through a series of experiments that test different strategies of randomized smoothing. We show that our approach can consistently improve prediction robustness of multiple base trajectory prediction models in various datasets without compromising accuracy in non-adversarial settings. Our results demonstrate that randomized smoothing offers a simple and computationally inexpensive technique for mitigating adversarial attacks in trajectory prediction.

### [108] [SNPgen: Phenotype-Supervised Genotype Representation and Synthetic Data Generation via Latent Diffusion](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.10873)
*Andrea Lampis,Michela Carlotta Massi,Nicola Pirastu,Francesca Ieva,Matteo Matteucci,Emanuele Di Angelantonio*

  <summary>Details</summary>

Conclusion: SNPgen成功地在保护隐私与保持下游分析效用之间取得了平衡，为受限基因组数据的共享与利用提供了一种有效的解决方案，生成的合成数据在预测性能和统计特性方面均表现优异。

Abstract: Polygenic risk scores and other genomic analyses require large individual-level genotype datasets, yet strict data access restrictions impede sharing. Synthetic genotype generation offers a privacy-preserving alternative, but most existing methods operate unconditionally, producing samples without phenotype alignment, or rely on unsupervised compression, creating a gap between statistical fidelity and downstream task utility. We present SNPgen, a two-stage conditional latent diffusion framework for generating phenotype-supervised synthetic genotypes. SNPgen combines GWAS-guided variant selection (1,024-2,048 trait-associated SNPs) with a variational autoencoder for genotype compression and a latent diffusion model conditioned on binary disease labels via classifier-free guidance. Evaluated on 458,724 UK Biobank individuals across four complex diseases (coronary artery disease, breast cancer, type 1 and type 2 diabetes), models trained on synthetic data matched real-data predictive performance in a train-on-synthetic, test-on-real protocol, approaching genome-wide PRS methods that use $2$-$6\times$ more variants. Privacy analysis confirmed zero identical matches, near-random membership inference (AUC $\approx 0.50$), preserved linkage disequilibrium structure, and high allele frequency correlation ($r \geq 0.95$) with source data. A controlled simulation with known causal effects verified faithful recovery of the imposed genetic association structure.

*Johannes Burchert,Ahmad Bdeir,Tom Hanika,Lars Schmidt-Thieme,Niels Landwehr*

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出LAtte框架，包含两个核心组件：（1）通过预训练任务学习所有被试共享的基线信号，捕获共同潜在模式；（2）利用新型洛伦兹低秩适配器学习被试特定嵌入，建模个体差异，从而构建跨被试鲁棒的共享模型。

Abstract: Electroencephalogram (EEG) classification is critical for applications ranging from medical diagnostics to brain-computer interfaces, yet it remains challenging due to the inherently low signal-to-noise ratio (SNR) and high inter-subject variability. To address these issues, we propose LAtte, a novel framework that integrates a Lorentz Attention Module with an InceptionTime-based encoder to enable robust and generalizable EEG classification. Unlike prior work, which evaluates primarily on single-subject performance, LAtte focuses on cross-subject training. First, we learn a shared baseline signal across all subjects using pretraining tasks to capture common underlying patterns. Then, we utilize novel Lorentz low-rank adapters to learn subject-specific embeddings that model individual differences. This allows us to learn a shared model that performs robustly across subjects, and can be subsequently finetuned for individual subjects or used to generalize to unseen subjects. We evaluate LAtte on three well-established EEG datasets, achieving a substantial improvement in performance over current state-of-the-art methods.

### [110] [Ergodicity in reinforcement learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.10895)
*Dominik Baumann,Erfaun Noorani,Arsenii Mustafin,Xinyi Sheng,Bert Verbruggen,Arne Vanhoyweghen,Vincent Ginis,Thomas B. Schön*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文指出在强化学习中，当奖励过程是非遍历的（non-ergodic）时，传统的期望值优化目标无法反映单个智能体在长期运行中的实际表现，因此需要采用替代优化目标。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在传统强化学习中，目标通常是最大化轨迹上奖励总和的期望值。然而，当奖励生成过程是非遍历的时，期望值（即无限多轨迹的平均）对于单个无限长轨迹的平均表现缺乏信息价值。由于实际部署中关注的是单个智能体的表现，期望值并非合适的优化目标。

Method: 本文通过一个启发性示例讨论非遍历奖励过程对强化学习智能体的影响，将遍历奖励过程的概念与更广泛使用的遍历马尔可夫链概念联系起来，并回顾现有的能够在非遍历奖励动态下优化个体轨迹长期性能的解决方案。

Result: 揭示了非遍历奖励过程下传统期望值优化的局限性，阐明了遍历性在强化学习中的重要性，并梳理了针对非遍历场景的替代优化方法。

Conclusion: 在非遍历奖励环境下，应采用能够优化个体轨迹长期表现的替代目标，而非传统期望值，以确保智能体在实际部署中的有效性。

Abstract: In reinforcement learning, we typically aim to optimize the expected value of the sum of rewards an agent collects over a trajectory. However, if the process generating these rewards is non-ergodic, the expected value, i.e., the average over infinitely many trajectories with a given policy, is uninformative for the average over a single, but infinitely long trajectory. Thus, if we care about how the individual agent performs during deployment, the expected value is not a good optimization objective. In this paper, we discuss the impact of non-ergodic reward processes on reinforcement learning agents through an instructive example, relate the notion of ergodic reward processes to more widely used notions of ergodic Markov chains, and present existing solutions that optimize long-term performance of individual trajectories under non-ergodic reward dynamics.

</details>

### [112] [ECoLAD: Deployment-Oriented Evaluation for Automotive Time-Series Anomaly Detection](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.10926)
*Kadir-Kaan Özer,René Ebeling,Markus Enzweiler*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出ECoLAD评估协议，通过单调计算缩减阶梯和显式CPU线程限制，在约束条件下评估时序异常检测器。实验表明在车载遥测数据上，轻量级经典检测器在保证延迟约束的同时维持检测性能，而部分深度学习方法在失去精度前就已失去部署可行性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有时序异常检测器基准测试主要关注准确率，在工作站级硬件和无约束环境下进行，忽略了车载部署场景中对可预测延迟和有限CPU并行性的实际约束。仅关注准确率的排行榜可能误导对方法部署可行性的判断。

Method: 提出ECoLAD（Efficiency Compute Ladder for Anomaly Detection）部署导向评估协议：1) 对异构检测器族应用单调计算缩减阶梯；2) 使用机械确定的整数缩放规则和显式CPU线程限制；3) 记录所有配置变更；4) 通过扫掠目标评分率，计算覆盖度（满足目标的实体比例）和满足约束条件下的最佳AUC-PR。在私有车载遥测数据（异常率≈0.022）和公共基准上进行实证研究。

Result: 在受限车载遥测数据上：1) 轻量级经典检测器在整个吞吐量扫掠范围内均能维持覆盖度和高于随机基线的检测提升；2) 若干深度学习方法在失去精度之前就已失去部署可行性（无法满足延迟约束）。这表明仅关注准确率的评估会高估部分深度方法的实用价值。

Conclusion: 准确率导向的排行榜不能反映方法在部署约束下的真实表现。ECoLAD协议通过显式建模计算约束，揭示了经典方法在资源受限场景下的优势，为实际部署提供了更可靠的方法选择依据。评估应同时考虑准确率和计算效率，以准确反映方法的部署可行性。

Abstract: Time-series anomaly detectors are commonly compared on workstation-class hardware under unconstrained execution. In-vehicle monitoring, however, requires predictable latency and stable behavior under limited CPU parallelism. Accuracy-only leaderboards can therefore misrepresent which methods remain feasible under deployment-relevant constraints.
  We present ECoLAD (Efficiency Compute Ladder for Anomaly Detection), a deployment-oriented evaluation protocol instantiated as an empirical study on proprietary automotive telemetry (anomaly rate ${\approx}$0.022) and complementary public benchmarks. ECoLAD applies a monotone compute-reduction ladder across heterogeneous detector families using mechanically determined, integer-only scaling rules and explicit CPU thread caps, while logging every applied configuration change. Throughput-constrained behavior is characterized by sweeping target scoring rates and reporting (i) coverage (the fraction of entities meeting the target) and (ii) the best AUC-PR achievable among measured ladder configurations satisfying the target. On constrained automotive telemetry, lightweight classical detectors sustain both coverage and detection lift above the random baseline across the full throughput sweep. Several deep methods lose feasibility before they lose accuracy.

### [113] [Quantifying Membership Disclosure Risk for Tabular Synthetic Data Using Kernel Density Estimators](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.10937)
*Rajdeep Pathak,Sayantee Jana*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于核密度估计器（KDE）的实用方法，用于量化表格合成数据集中的成员披露风险，通过建模合成数据与训练记录之间的最近邻距离分布，实现了对成员推断攻击的有效评估，在多个数据集和生成器上均优于现有基线方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 合成数据作为隐私保护的替代方案在医疗、金融等敏感领域日益普及，但其隐私保证并非绝对，仍面临成员推断攻击（MIAs）的威胁。现有方法缺乏实用且有效的风险评估框架，因此需要一种能够量化成员披露风险的实用方法。

Method: 提出基于核密度估计器（KDE）的方法，建模合成数据与训练记录之间的最近邻距离分布，实现成员身份的概率推断。设计了两种攻击模型：假设拥有训练数据特权访问的"真实分布攻击"和更现实的、使用辅助数据且无需真实成员标签的"现实攻击"。通过ROC曲线实现稳健评估。

Result: 在四个真实世界数据集和六个合成数据生成器上的实证评估表明，该方法在F1分数和风险刻画方面始终优于先前的基线方法，且无需计算昂贵的影子模型。方法提供了实用的框架和度量标准，使数据管理者能够在发布合成数据集之前进行生成后风险评估。

Conclusion: 所提出的KDE方法为合成数据中的成员披露风险量化提供了实用框架，使数据管理者能够在发布合成数据集之前进行风险评估，为下游使用提供安全保障。

Abstract: The use of synthetic data has become increasingly popular as a privacy-preserving alternative to sharing real datasets, especially in sensitive domains such as healthcare, finance, and demography. However, the privacy assurances of synthetic data are not absolute, and remain susceptible to membership inference attacks (MIAs), where adversaries aim to determine whether a specific individual was present in the dataset used to train the generator. In this work, we propose a practical and effective method to quantify membership disclosure risk in tabular synthetic datasets using kernel density estimators (KDEs). Our KDE-based approach models the distribution of nearest-neighbour distances between synthetic data and the training records, allowing probabilistic inference of membership and enabling robust evaluation via ROC curves. We propose two attack models: a 'True Distribution Attack', which assumes privileged access to training data, and a more realistic, implementable 'Realistic Attack' that uses auxiliary data without true membership labels. Empirical evaluations across four real-world datasets and six synthetic data generators demonstrate that our method consistently achieves higher F1 scores and sharper risk characterization than a prior baseline approach, without requiring computationally expensive shadow models. The proposed method provides a practical framework and metric for quantifying membership disclosure risk in synthetic data, which enables data custodians to conduct a post-generation risk assessment prior to releasing their synthetic datasets for downstream use. The datasets and codes for this study are available at https://github.com/PyCoder913/MIA-KDE.

</details>


### [114] [When should we trust the annotation? Selective prediction for molecular structure retrieval from mass spectra](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.10950)
*Mira Jürgens,Gaetan De Waele,Morteza Rakhshaninejad,Willem Waegeman*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了一个针对质谱分子结构检索的选择性预测框架，允许模型在不确定性过高时拒绝预测。研究发现，一阶置信度量和检索层面的偶然不确定性在风险-覆盖率权衡中表现优异，并可通过分布自由风险控制实现可容忍错误率的设定。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的机器学习方法在从串联质谱（MS/MS）识别分子结构时仍存在显著错误率。在临床代谢组学和环境筛查等高风险应用中，错误注释可能导致严重后果，因此确定何时可以信任模型预测至关重要。

Method: 提出一个选择性预测框架，在风险-覆盖率权衡框架下建模。在两个粒度层面（指纹层面的分子指纹位不确定性和检索层面的候选排序不确定性）全面评估不确定性量化策略。比较了多种评分函数，包括一阶置信度度量、来自二阶分布的偶然和认知不确定性估计，以及潜在空间中的距离度量。在MassSpecGym基准上进行实验。

Result: 指纹层面的不确定性分数不能很好地代表检索成功与否；计算成本低的一阶置信度量和检索层面的偶然不确定性在各评估设置中实现了强大的风险-覆盖率权衡。通过应用分布自由风险控制（通过泛化界限），实践者可以指定可容忍的错误率，并获得以高概率满足该约束的注释子集。

Conclusion: 该框架使实践者能够在高风险应用中有效控制错误率，通过设定可容忍错误率来获得可靠的注释子集，从而提高分子结构注释的可信度。

Abstract: Machine learning methods for identifying molecular structures from tandem mass spectra (MS/MS) have advanced rapidly, yet current approaches still exhibit significant error rates. In high-stakes applications such as clinical metabolomics and environmental screening, incorrect annotations can have serious consequences, making it essential to determine when a prediction can be trusted. We introduce a selective prediction framework for molecular structure retrieval from MS/MS spectra, enabling models to abstain from predictions when uncertainty is too high. We formulate the problem within the risk-coverage tradeoff framework and comprehensively evaluate uncertainty quantification strategies at two levels of granularity: fingerprint-level uncertainty over predicted molecular fingerprint bits, and retrieval-level uncertainty over candidate rankings. We compare scoring functions including first-order confidence measures, aleatoric and epistemic uncertainty estimates from second-order distributions, as well as distance-based measures in the latent space. All experiments are conducted on the MassSpecGym benchmark. Our analysis reveals that while fingerprint-level uncertainty scores are poor proxies for retrieval success, computationally inexpensive first-order confidence measures and retrieval-level aleatoric uncertainty achieve strong risk-coverage tradeoffs across evaluation settings. We demonstrate that by applying distribution-free risk control via generalization bounds, practitioners can specify a tolerable error rate and obtain a subset of annotations satisfying that constraint with high probability.

Using greedy decoding as an empirical prior ($\mathrm{Bayes}_{\mathbf{R}_0}@N$) reduces variance at $N=1$ by $16$--$52\%$, but can bias rankings when greedy and stochastic sampling disagree. ### [120] [The Discrete Charm of the MLP: Binary Routing of Continuous Signals in Transformer Feed-Forward Layers](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.10985)
*Peter Balogh*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文揭示了Transformer语言模型中MLP层的二元路由机制：特定神经元通过二元激活决策令牌是否需要非线性处理，形成共识架构（7个默认开启神经元+1个异常处理器），在完整共识下移除MLP仅导致10.1%困惑度损失，而在共识崩溃时损失达43.3%。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解Transformer模型中MLP层的计算功能，解释为何光滑多项式近似在高度非线性层上失效（R²≤0.06），揭示深度网络沿自然数据流形的分段边界如何实现二元路由决策。

Method: 在GPT-2 Small（124M参数）上分析神经元激活模式，识别共识架构（7个默认开启神经元和1个异常处理器N2123），进行跨层分析（L1-11）以追踪发育轨迹，并通过因果验证（移除MLP测量困惑度变化）和二元vs连续特征对比来验证路由机制。

Result: 发现GPT-2 Small中Layer 11存在93-98%互斥的二元路由开关；跨层分析显示发育弧线：早期层（L1-3）使用单一网关神经元，中期层（L4-6）呈扩散处理，晚期层（L7-11）形成完整共识/异常架构；二元化仅损失0.4%准确率（79.2% vs 78.8%），但连续激活携带额外幅度信息（R²=0.36 vs 0.22）。

Conclusion: 深度网络的分段仿射表征可由路由表征补充：沿自然数据流形，分段边界实现关于哪些令牌需要非线性处理的二元决策，将连续信号通过性质不同的计算路径进行路由。

Abstract: We show that MLP layers in transformer language models perform binary routing of continuous signals: the decision of whether a token needs nonlinear processing is well-captured by binary neuron activations, even though the signals being routed are continuous. In GPT-2 Small (124M parameters), we find that specific neurons implement a consensus architecture -- seven "default-ON" neurons and one exception handler (N2123 in Layer 11) that are 93-98% mutually exclusive -- creating a binary routing switch. A cross-layer analysis reveals a developmental arc: early layers (L1-3) use single gateway neurons to route exceptions without consensus quorums; middle layers (L4-6) show diffuse processing with neither gateway nor consensus; and late layers (L7-11) crystallize full consensus/exception architectures with increasing quorum size (1 to 3 to 7 consensus neurons). Causal validation confirms the routing is functional: removing the MLP at consensus breakdown costs 43.3% perplexity, while at full consensus removing it costs only 10.1% -- exceeding a 4x difference. Comparing binary vs. continuous features for the routing decision confirms that binarization loses essentially no information (79.2% vs. 78.8% accuracy), while continuous activations carry additional magnitude information (R^2 = 0.36 vs. 0.22). This binary routing structure explains why smooth polynomial approximation fails: cross-validated polynomial fits (degrees 2-7) never exceed R^2 = 0.06 for highly nonlinear layers. We propose that the well-established piecewise-affine characterization of deep networks can be complemented by a routing characterization: along the natural data manifold, the piecewise boundaries implement binary decisions about which tokens need nonlinear processing, routing continuous signals through qualitatively different computational paths.

</details>


### [121] [MCMC Informed Neural Emulators for Uncertainty Quantification in Dynamical Systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.10987)
*Heikki Haario,Zhi-Song Liu,Martin Simon,Hendrik Weichel*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 提出了一种将不确定性量化与神经网络架构解耦的方法，通过MCMC将模型参数分布作为网络训练的输入，而非采样网络权重，从而在大幅减少计算时间的同时实现与底层物理模型相同的不确定性量化。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统的参数化不确定性量化方法需要准确的模型参数先验分布，而在实际中，直接筛选或随机采样模型参数会导致训练时间过长，并且会在非物理参数值上进行评估，效率低下。

Method: 将不确定性量化与神经网络架构解耦，不再采样网络权重，而是通过马尔可夫链蒙特卡洛（MCMC）方法将模型参数分布作为网络训练的输入。该方法对神经网络的选择完全无关。

Result: 该方法在示例中展示了用于预测的分位数模拟器和一个新颖的基于自编码器的ODE网络模拟器，能够灵活估计对应不同ODE模型参数的不同轨迹路径。同时提供了数学分析，将潜在性能损失与可测量的分布不匹配相关联。

Conclusion: 该方法成功地实现了代理模型与底层物理模型相同的不确定性量化，同时大幅减少了计算时间，并且与神经网络的选择无关，提供了一种透明的方式来评估性能损失。

Abstract: Neural networks are a commonly used approach to replace physical models with computationally cheap surrogates. Parametric uncertainty quantification can be included in training, assuming that an accurate prior distribution of the model parameters is available. Here we study the common opposite situation, where direct screening or random sampling of model parameters leads to exhaustive training times and evaluations at unphysical parameter values. Our solution is to decouple uncertainty quantification from network architecture. Instead of sampling network weights, we introduce the model-parameter distribution as an input to network training via Markov chain Monte Carlo (MCMC). In this way, the surrogate achieves the same uncertainty quantification as the underlying physical model, but with substantially reduced computation time. The approach is fully agnostic with respect to the neural network choice. In our examples, we present a quantile emulator for prediction and a novel autoencoder-based ODE network emulator that can flexibly estimate different trajectory paths corresponding to different ODE model parameters. Moreover, we present a mathematical analysis that provides a transparent way to relate potential performance loss to measurable distribution mismatch.

### [122] [Factorized Neural Implicit DMD for Parametric Dynamics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.10995)
*Siyuan Chen,Zhecheng Wang,Yixin Chen,Yue Chang,Peter Yichen Chen,Eitan Grinspun,Jonathan Panuelos*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种物理编码神经场方法来参数化Koopman算子的谱分解，通过解耦空间模态和时间演化，实现对动力系统的长期预测、参数泛化和谱分析。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统的物理建模方法依赖已知控制方程，且在高维非线性系统中计算成本高昂，难以满足实时分析和控制需求。数据驱动的无模型方法虽能缓解对显式方程的依赖，但现有方法（如物理约束神经场和神经算子）在长期预测、参数泛化和谱分析方面存在局限。因此需要一种新方法来学习动力系统的参数化流，支持长时间预测、参数空间泛化和谱分析。

Method: 提出物理编码神经场（physics-coded neural field）来参数化Koopman算子的谱分解。与仅拟合单一解曲面的物理约束神经场和固定时间视界直接逼近解算子的神经算子不同，该方法学习一个因子化流算子，将空间模态与时间演化解耦。这种结构能够暴露底层的特征值、模态和物理过程的稳定性，从而支持稳定的长期预测、跨参数空间插值和谱分析。

Result: 在多个动力学问题上验证了方法的有效性，能够准确预测复杂的时空现象，同时提供对系统动态行为的洞察。模型展示了稳定的长期预测能力、对未见参数的良好泛化性，以及有效的谱分析能力。

Conclusion: 通过将Koopman算子的谱分解与神经场表示相结合，所提出的物理编码神经场方法成功实现了空间模态与时间演化的解耦，为动力系统的建模提供了可解释、稳定且可泛化的解决方案，在复杂时空现象预测和动力学行为分析方面展现出显著优势。

Abstract: A data-driven, model-free approach to modeling the temporal evolution of physical systems mitigates the need for explicit knowledge of the governing equations. Even when physical priors such as partial differential equations are available, such systems often reside in high-dimensional state spaces and exhibit nonlinear dynamics, making traditional numerical solvers computationally expensive and ill-suited for real-time analysis and control. Consider the problem of learning a parametric flow of a dynamical system: with an initial field and a set of physical parameters, we aim to predict the system's evolution over time in a way that supports long-horizon rollouts, generalization to unseen parameters, and spectral analysis.
  We propose a physics-coded neural field parameterization of the Koopman operator's spectral decomposition. Unlike a physics-constrained neural field, which fits a single solution surface, and neural operators, which directly approximate the solution operator at fixed time horizons, our model learns a factorized flow operator that decouples spatial modes and temporal evolution. This structure exposes underlying eigenvalues, modes, and stability of the underlying physical process to enable stable long-term rollouts, interpolation across parameter spaces, and spectral analysis. We demonstrate the efficacy of our method on a range of dynamics problems, showcasing its ability to accurately predict complex spatiotemporal phenomena while providing insights into the system's dynamic behavior.

</details>


### [123] [Cross-Species Transfer Learning for Electrophysiology-to-Transcriptomics Mapping in Cortical GABAergic Interneurons](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.11000)
*Theo Schwider,Ramin Ramezani*

TL;DR: 本研究复现并扩展了Gouwens等人(2020)的电生理-转录组关联框架，使用注意力机制BiLSTM序列模型直接处理IPFX特征表示，并通过小鼠到人类的迁移学习提升了人类皮层GABAergic抑制性中间神经元亚型预测的性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 单细胞电生理记录为理解神经元功能多样性提供了有力工具，能够建立内在生理特性与转录组身份之间的可解释联系。本研究旨在复现并扩展现有的电生理-转录组关联框架，探索跨物种迁移学习在神经元亚型分类中的潜力。

Conclusion: 研究结果证实了Gouwens流程在小鼠数据上的可重复性，证明序列模型可以达到特征工程基线的性能水平，并展示了小鼠到人类迁移学习能够为人类神经元亚型预测提供可测量的性能增益。

Abstract: Single-cell electrophysiological recordings provide a powerful window into neuronal functional diversity and offer an interpretable route for linking intrinsic physiology to transcriptomic identity. Here, we replicate and extend the electrophysiology-to-transcriptomics framework introduced by Gouwens et al. (2020) using publicly available Allen Institute Patch-seq datasets from both mouse and human cortex. We focus on GABAergic inhibitory interneurons to target a subclass structure (Lamp5, Pvalb, Sst, Vip) that is comparable and conserved across species. After quality control, we analyzed 3,699 mouse visual cortex neurons and 506 human neocortical neurons from neurosurgical resections. Using standardized electrophysiological features and sparse PCA, we reproduced the major class-level separations reported in the original mouse study. For supervised prediction, a class-balanced random forest provided a strong feature-engineered baseline in mouse data and a reduced but still informative baseline in human data. We then developed an attention-based BiLSTM that operates directly on the structured IPFX feature-family representation, avoiding sPCA and providing feature-family-level interpretability via learned attention weights. Finally, we evaluated a cross-species transfer setting in which the sequence model is pretrained on mouse data and fine-tuned on human data for an aligned 4-class task, improving human macro-F1 relative to a human-only training baseline. Together, these results confirm reproducibility of the Gouwens pipeline in mouse data, demonstrate that sequence models can match feature-engineered baselines, and show that mouse-to-human transfer learning can provide measurable gains for human subclass prediction.

### [124] [Leech Lattice Vector Quantization for Efficient LLM Compression](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.11021)
*Tycho F. A. van der Ouderaa,Mart van Baalen,Paul Whatmough,Markus Nagel*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了Leech格向量量化(LLVQ)方法，利用24维Leech格的最优球填充特性，实现了大语言模型的先进量化性能，无需显式码本存储即可完成编解码。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大语言模型的标量量化受限于信息论界限，而传统向量量化方法需要昂贵的查找机制或显式码本存储。本文旨在利用具有最优球填充和接吻配置的高维格结构(Leech格)来解决这些限制，实现无需码本的实用化向量量化方案。

Method: 基于扩展Golay码构造的搜索算法进行扩展：i)支持索引功能，实现在不实例化码本的情况下与比特串的双向转换；ii)允许在Leech格壳的并集上进行角度搜索；iii)提出完全可并行的去量化核函数。最终形成Leech格向量量化(LLVQ)算法。

Result: LLVQ在大语言模型量化任务上达到了最先进的性能，超越了Quip#、QTIP和PVQ等近期方法，验证了高维格结构在可扩展、理论基础扎实的模型压缩中的重要性。

Conclusion: 高维格结构特别是Leech格，为大语言模型的可扩展且具有理论基础的压缩提供了有效途径，证明了向量量化在高维空间中的优越性。

Abstract: Scalar quantization of large language models (LLMs) is fundamentally limited by information-theoretic bounds. While vector quantization (VQ) overcomes these limits by encoding blocks of parameters jointly, practical implementations must avoid the need for expensive lookup mechanisms or other explicit codebook storage. Lattice approaches address this through highly structured and dense packing. This paper explores the Leech lattice, which, with its optimal sphere packing and kissing configurations at 24 dimensions, is the highest dimensional lattice known with such optimal properties. To make the Leech lattice usable for LLM quantization, we extend an existing search algorithm based on the extended Golay code construction, to i) support indexing, enabling conversion to and from bitstrings without materializing the codebook, ii) allow angular search over union of Leech lattice shells, iii) propose fully-parallelisable dequantization kernel. Together this yields a practical algorithm, namely Leech Lattice Vector Quantization (LLVQ). LLVQ delivers state-of-the-art LLM quantization performance, outperforming recent methods such as Quip\#, QTIP, and PVQ. These results highlight the importance of high-dimensional lattices for scalable, theoretically grounded model compression.

</details>

### [125] [RedFuser: An Automatic Operator Fusion Framework for Cascaded Reductions on AI Accelerators](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.10026)
*Xinsheng Tang,Yangcheng Li,Nan Wang,Zhiyi Shu,Xingyu Ling,Junna Xing,Peng Zhou,Qiang Liu*

Main category: cs.AR

TL;DR: 本文提出了RedFuser框架，通过形式化理论方法自动识别和融合级联归约操作，解决了现有AI编译器无法有效处理此类模式的问题，实现了2-5倍的加速。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有AI编译器对于包含跨循环数据依赖的级联归约操作（如注意力机制中的safe softmax后接GEMM）缺乏有效的自动融合和内核生成能力。虽然有手工优化的解决方案，但其通用性有限且难以扩展。鉴于此类计算模式在深度学习模型中广泛存在，存在巨大的优化潜力尚未挖掘。

Method: 提出了一种形式化理论方法来分析级联归约操作，能够将其融合为单个循环并引入增量计算形式。基于该方法论设计了RedFuser框架，能够自动识别支持的级联归约模式并生成优化的融合内核。

Result: 实验表明RedFuser成功融合了多种工作负载，相比最先进的AI编译器实现了2倍到5倍的加速，性能与高度优化的手写内核相当。

Conclusion: RedFuser为级联归约操作提供了一种通用且自动化的融合优化方案，填补了现有AI编译器在此类计算模式优化方面的空白，显著提升了深度学习模型的执行效率。

Abstract: Operator fusion, as a key performance optimization technique in the deployment of AI models, significantly improves execution efficiency and has been widely adopted in modern AI compilers. However, for cascaded reduction operations involving multiple loops with inter-loop data dependencies, such as the safe softmax followed by GEMM within attention mechanisms, existing compilers lack effective automated fusion and kernel generation capabilities. Although some works have addressed specific instances through hand-crafted fusion strategies, their solutions are limited in generality and difficult to extend to other similar structures. Given the prevalence of such computational patterns in deep learning models, there remains significant untapped potential in achieving general and automated fusion optimization.
  In this paper, we present a formal theoretical methodology for analyzing cascaded reductions which can fuse them into a single loop and introduce an incremental computation form. Based on this methodology, we design Reduction Fuser (RedFuser), a framework that automatically identifies supported cascaded reduction patterns and generates optimized fused kernels. Experiments show that RedFuser successfully fuses diverse workloads, achieving up to 2$\times$ to 5$\times$ speedup over state-of-the-art AI compilers and matching the performance of highly optimized hand-written kernels. The code is available at https://github.com/alibaba/redfuser

Abstract: As LLM agents evolve into collaborative multi-agent systems, their memory requirements grow rapidly in complexity. We distinguish shared and distributed memory paradigms, propose a three-layer memory hierarchy (I/O, cache, and memory), and identify two critical protocol gaps: cache sharing across agents and structured memory access control. We argue that the most pressing open challenge is multi-agent memory consistency. Our architectural framing provides a foundation for building reliable, scalable multi-agent systems.

### [127] [The DMA Streaming Framework: Kernel-Level Buffer Orchestration for High-Performance AI Data Paths](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.10030)
*Marco Graziano*

Main category: cs.AR

TL;DR: 本文提出了dmaplane，一个Linux内核模块，将AI传输库中隐含的缓冲区管理层显式化为缓冲区编排层，通过统一的内核UAPI提供DMA缓冲区生命周期管理、跨设备共享、RDMA引擎、NUMA感知分配、流控及GPU内存集成等功能，有效解决了缓冲区分配、放置、共享、注册及安全性问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有AI传输库能够高效移动数据字节，但普遍假设缓冲区已正确分配、放置、共享、注册，且在完成和拆解压力下保持安全，缺少显式的缓冲区编排层，导致开发者需要手动处理复杂的底层细节。

Method: 设计并实现dmaplane Linux内核模块，通过/dev/dmaplane暴露稳定的内核UAPI，集成基于环形缓冲区的命令通道、DMA缓冲区生命周期管理、dma-buf跨设备导出、内核空间RDMA引擎、NUMA感知分配与验证、基于信用的流控机制、低开销可观测性，以及通过PCIe BAR pinning实现GPU内存集成。

Result: 通过测量NUMA跨节点访问惩罚（DRAM规模）、持续RDMA负载下的完成安全流控、GPU BAR映射层级与cudaMemcpy的性能对比，验证了编排敏感性；演示了端到端 disaggregated inference 场景下，使用RDMA WRITE WITH IMMEDIATE在两台机器间传输KV-cache块并在接收端重构张量视图。

Conclusion: dmaplane成功将缓冲区编排作为独立层面显式化，为AI传输库提供了统一、可靠、高性能的底层基础设施支持，有效简化了跨设备、跨节点数据传输的复杂度，并为disaggregated inference等应用场景提供了可行方案。

Abstract: AI transport libraries move bytes efficiently, but they commonly assume that buffers are already correctly allocated, placed, shared, registered, and safe under completion and teardown pressure. This paper presents dmaplane, a Linux kernel module that makes this missing layer explicit as buffer orchestration. dmaplane exposes a stable kernel UAPI via /dev/dmaplane and composes ring-based command channels, DMA buffer lifecycle management, dma-buf export for cross-device sharing, a kernel-space RDMA engine, NUMA-aware allocation and verification, credit-based flow control, low-overhead observability, and GPU memory integration via PCIe BAR pinning. We evaluate orchestration sensitivity with measurements of NUMA cross-node penalties at DRAM scale, completion-safe flow control under sustained RDMA load, and GPU BAR mapping tiers versus cudaMemcpy. We also demonstrate end-to-end disaggregated inference by transferring KV-cache chunks between two machines using RDMA WRITE WITH IMMEDIATE and reconstructing tensor views on the receiver. RDMA measurements use Soft-RoCE; we distinguish measured results from provider-independent properties by construction.

### [128] [Architecture-Aware LLM Inference Optimization on AMD Instinct GPUs: A Comprehensive Benchmark and Deployment Study](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.10031)
*Athos Georgiou*

Main category: cs.AR

TL;DR: 本文在AMD Instinct MI325X GPU集群上对四种大语言模型（235B至1万亿参数）进行了跨架构推理性能评估，发现架构感知优化至关重要：MLA模型需特定配置且无法使用KV缓存卸载，而GQA模型可从中受益；AITER运行时对MLA推理吞吐量提升关键但对其他架构效果有限；所有模型在1000并发用户下保持100%成功率，处理了1890万token。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 随着大语言模型在生产环境中的广泛部署，不同架构（MoE、Dense、MLA、GQA）的模型在推理性能上存在显著差异。为了指导生产环境中的硬件选型和软件优化决策，需要系统性地评估不同架构模型在AMD GPU平台上的推理性能特征，特别是架构感知优化策略的有效性。

Method: 在8卡AMD Instinct MI325X GPU集群（总计2TB HBM3e显存）上，使用vLLM v0.14.1框架对四种模型进行基准测试：涵盖三种架构组合（MoE+MLA、Dense+GQA、MoE+GQA），参数规模从235B到1万亿。通过控制变量实验评估AITER运行时的效果（n=5），测试纯文本和视觉工作负载下的吞吐量，并分析不同并发级别下的性能表现。

Result: MLA模型需要block size 1且无法使用KV缓存卸载，GQA模型则可从两者受益；AITER对Llama-3.1-405B仅有3-5%吞吐提升但测量变异性增加2-16倍，主要加速MoE/MLA内核。纯文本工作负载下Llama-405B与DeepSeek V3.2峰值吞吐相当（15,944 vs 15,343 tok/s）；视觉工作负载下Qwen3-VL-235B吞吐量是Kimi-K2.5的6.5倍。所有模型在约500并发（短序列）或100-200并发（长序列）时达到吞吐饱和，呈现内存带宽瓶颈特征。

Conclusion: 架构感知优化对生产环境LLM推理至关重要，不同架构需要定制化的优化策略。AITER运行时应针对MoE/MLA架构选择性启用。每token活跃参数数量与推理吞吐量相关，但受量化、加速和并行度等因素影响。所有测试模型在1000并发用户下保持100% HTTP成功率，验证了系统的稳定性。

Abstract: We present a cross-architecture evaluation of production LLM inference on AMD Instinct MI325X GPUs, benchmarking four models spanning 235B to 1 trillion parameters across three architectural families (MoE+MLA, Dense+GQA, MoE+GQA) on an 8-GPU cluster with 2TB aggregate HBM3e using vLLM v0.14.1. Our results demonstrate that architecture-aware optimization is essential: MLA models require block size 1 and cannot use KV cache offloading, while GQA models benefit from both. The AMD AITER runtime is required for competitive MLA inference throughput and must be selectively disabled for architectures with incompatible attention head configurations. A controlled AITER ablation on Llama-3.1-405B (n=5 per condition) reveals a modest 3-5% throughput benefit at high concurrency but 2-16x higher measurement variability, confirming that AITER's large speedups target MoE/MLA kernels specifically. Under text-only workloads, Llama-405B and DeepSeek V3.2 achieve comparable peak throughput (15,944 and 15,343 tok/s) despite an order-of-magnitude difference in active parameters. Under vision workloads, Qwen3-VL-235B reaches 47,873 tok/s, 6.5x higher than Kimi-K2.5 (7,327 tok/s). Active parameter count per token is associated with inference throughput, though confounded by differences in quantization, AITER acceleration, and tensor parallelism. All four models exhibit a common throughput saturation point consistent with a memory-bandwidth bottleneck (~500 concurrent for short sequences, ~100-200 for longer sequences). All models maintain 100% HTTP-level success rates through 1,000 concurrent users, processing 18.9 million tokens across 17,406 requests without failures.

### [129] [HTM-EAR: Importance-Preserving Tiered Memory with Hybrid Routing under Saturation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.10032)
*Shubham Kumar Singh*

Main category: cs.AR

TL;DR: 本文提出HTM-EAR，一种分层记忆管理系统，通过结合基于HNSW的工作记忆(L1)和档案存储(L2)，使用重要性感知的淘汰机制和混合路由策略，在有限上下文限制下有效管理长期运行代理的累积事实，在饱和状态下保持了高查询精度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 长期运行的智能代理在有限上下文限制下面临记忆管理挑战，需要在约束条件下对累积的事实进行结构化管理，同时保留关键信息并遗忘过时历史。

Method: 提出分层分级记忆架构HTM-EAR：(1)L1工作记忆基于HNSW构建，容量有限；(2)L2档案存储提供更大容量；(3)L1满时根据重要性和使用频率加权评分进行淘汰；(4)查询优先在L1执行，若相似度或实体覆盖不足则回退到L2，并使用交叉编码器重排序候选结果。

Result: 在饱和场景(15000事实，L1容量500，L2容量5000)测试中：(1)完整模型保持查询精度MRR=1.000，接近无界oracle性能(0.997±0.003)；(2)LRU虽延迟最低(21.1ms)但永久丢失2416个关键事实；(3)BGL日志测试中，完整系统MRR=0.336(接近oracle的0.370)，LRU仅0.069。消融实验验证了交叉编码器重排序和路由门控的重要性。

Conclusion: HTM-EAR通过分层记忆架构和重要性感知的淘汰机制，成功在有限上下文约束下平衡了信息保留与遗忘，显著优于传统LRU策略，为长期运行代理的记忆管理提供了有效解决方案。

Abstract: Memory constraints in long-running agents require structured management of accumulated facts while preserving essential information under bounded context limits. We introduce HTM-EAR, a hierarchical tiered memory substrate that integrates HNSW-based working memory (L1) with archival storage (L2), combining importance-aware eviction and hybrid routing. When L1 reaches capacity, items are evicted using a weighted score of importance and usage. Queries are first resolved in L1; if similarity or entity coverage is insufficient, retrieval falls back to L2, and candidates are re-ranked using a cross-encoder.
  We evaluate the system under sustained saturation (15,000 facts; L1 capacity 500; L2 capacity 5000) using synthetic streams across five random seeds and real BGL system logs. Ablation studies compare the full system against variants without cross-encoder re-ranking, without routing gates, with LRU eviction, and an oracle with unbounded memory. Under saturation, the full model preserves active-query precision (MRR = 1.000) while enabling controlled forgetting of stale history, approaching oracle active performance (0.997 +/- 0.003). In contrast, LRU minimizes latency (21.1 ms) but permanently evicts 2416 essential facts. On BGL logs, the full system achieves MRR 0.336, close to the oracle (0.370), while LRU drops to 0.069. Code is publicly available at: https://github.com/shubham-61291/HTM-EAR

</details>


### [130] [Pooling Engram Conditional Memory in Large Language Models using CXL](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.10087)
*Ruiyang Ma,Teng Ma,Zhiyuan Su,Hantian Zha,Xinpeng Zhao,Xuchun Shang,Xingrui Yi,Zheng Liu,Zhu Cao,An Wu,Zhichong Dou,Ziqian Liu,Daikang Kuang,Guojie Luo*

Main category: cs.AR

TL;DR: 本文提出利用CXL内存池存储Engram条件记忆，相比RDMA提供更低延迟的细粒度访问，集成至SGLang后实现了接近DRAM的端到端性能，为LLM提供了可扩展且经济的存储方案。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Engram条件记忆通过解耦静态知识查找与动态计算成为LLM的有前途组件，其稀疏访问模式和支持预取的特性使其适合卸载到低层内存。现有的RDMA方案无法满足Engram最小化和离散检索模式所需的细粒度、低延迟访问需求。

Method: 提出使用Compute Express Link (CXL)内存池存储Engram。相比RDMA，CXL提供细粒度和低延迟访问能力，满足Engram的最小化和离散检索模式要求。将基于CXL的Engram池集成到SGLang框架中。

Result: 集成CXL-based Engram池的SGLang实现了接近DRAM的端到端性能，证明了该方案在保证推理性能的同时提供了可扩展且经济高效的存储解决方案。

Conclusion: CXL内存池作为Engram存储方案，能够在不牺牲推理性能的前提下，为未来集成Engram的LLM提供可扩展且具有成本效益的存储解决方案。

Abstract: Engram conditional memory has emerged as a promising component for LLMs by decoupling static knowledge lookup from dynamic computation. Since Engram exhibits sparse access patterns and supports prefetching, its massive embedding tables are well-suited for offloading to lower-tier memory. In this paper, we propose using Compute Express Link (CXL) memory pool for Engram storage. Compared to RDMA, CXL provides fine-grained and low-latency access required by minimal and discrete retrieval patterns of Engram. We integrate the CXL-based Engram pool into SGLang, achieving near-DRAM end-to-end performance. This provides a scalable and cost-efficient storage solution for future Engram-integrated LLMs without compromising inference performance.

</details>


### [131] [In-Memory ADC-Based Nonlinear Activation Quantization for Efficient In-Memory Computing](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.10540)
*Shuai Dong,Junyi Yang,Biyan Zhou,Hongyang Shang,Gourav Datta,Arindam Basu*

Main category: cs.AR

TL;DR: 本文提出了边界抑制K均值量化方法(BS-KMQ)，通过抑制激活值分布边界的离群点实现更优的非线性量化，在存内计算系统中显著降低了ADC分辨率需求并提升了量化精度和能效。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在深度神经网络中，ReLU等操作和硬件驱动的截断会导致激活值在分布边缘累积，造成聚类偏倚，使现有非线性量化方法效果不佳。现有方法无法有效处理这种边界偏倚问题，限制了存内计算系统中ADC的性能优化。

Method: 提出边界抑制K均值量化(BS-KMQ)方法：在聚类前先抑制边界离群点，从而获得更均衡且信息量更大的非线性量化层级；将生成的非线性参考值通过可重构存内非线性ADC实现硬件部署。

Result: 在ResNet-18、VGG-16、Inception-V3和DistilBERT上，BS-KMQ的量化误差比线性量化、Lloyd-Max、CDF和K-means方法降低至少3倍；相比线性量化，训练后量化精度分别提升66.8%、25.4%、66.6%和67.7%；系统级仿真显示比现有IMC加速器实现最高4倍加速和24倍能效提升。

Conclusion: BS-KMQ有效解决了激活值边界累积导致的量化偏倚问题，实现了低比特精度保持(3-4位NL-ADC层级)，面积优化7倍，为存内计算系统提供了高效的非线性量化解决方案。

Abstract: In deep networks, operations such as ReLU and hardware-driven clamping often cause activations to accumulate near the edges of the distribution, leading to biased clustering and suboptimal quantization in existing nonlinear (NL) quantization methods. This paper introduces Boundary Suppressed K-Means Quantization (BS-KMQ), a novel NL quantization approach designed to reduce the resolution requirements of analog-to-digital converters (ADCs) in in-memory computing (IMC) systems. By suppressing boundary outliers before clustering, BS-KMQ achieves more balanced and informative NL quantization levels. The resulting NL references are implemented using a reconfigurable in-memory NL-ADC, achieving a 7x area improvement over prior NL-ADC designs. When evaluated on ResNet-18, VGG-16, Inception-V3, and DistilBERT, BS-KMQ achieves at least 3x lower quantization error compared to linear, Lloyd-Max, cumulative distribution function (CDF), and K-means methods. It also improves post-training quantization accuracy by up to 66.8%, 25.4%, 66.6%, and 67.7%, respectively, compared to linear quantization. After low-bit fine-tuning, BS-KMQ maintains competitive accuracy with significantly fewer NL-ADC levels (3/3/4/4b). System-level simulations on ResNet-18 (6/2/3b) demonstrate up to a 4x speedup and 24x energy efficiency improvement over existing IMC accelerators.

</details>

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出了一种高效的流水线FPGA架构设计用于DV搜索模块，并引入优化的存储组织方案，充分利用IPC的计算特性和数据固有的重用模式来提升性能。

A key module of IPC is the displacement vector (DV) search, which aims to solve the optimal prediction reference offset. However, the DV search process is computationally intensive, posing challenges for practical hardware deployment. In this paper, we propose an efficient pipelined FPGA architecture design for the DV search module to promote the practical deployment of IPC. Optimized memory organization, which leverages the IPC computational characteristics and data inherent reuse patterns, is further introduced to enhance the performance. Experimental results show that our proposed architecture achieves a throughput of 38.3 Mpixels/s with a power consumption of 277 mW, demonstrating its feasibility for practical hardware implementation in IPC and other predictive coding tools, and providing a promising foundation for ASIC deployment.

To tackle this, we introduce LLMGreenRec, a novel multi-agent framework that leverages Large Language Models (LLMs) to promote sustainable consumption. Notably, this intent-driven approach also reduces unnecessary interactions and energy consumption. ### [134] [AgentServe: Algorithm-System Co-Design for Efficient Agentic AI Serving on a Consumer-Grade GPU](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.10342)
*Yuning Zhang,Yan Yan,Nan Yang,Dong Yuan*

Main category: cs.DC

TL;DR: 针对多AI代理在单GPU上的推理服务需求，提出了AgentServe系统，通过隔离预填充与解码阶段、动态预算控制和CUDA Green Context资源分配，解决了异构请求竞争导致的性能不稳定问题，显著提升了延迟稳定性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 随着大语言模型作为AI代理的部署增加，以及出于隐私和成本考虑向本地消费级GPU运行小语言模型的趋势，多代理工作负载在单GPU上产生异构请求竞争。长预填充与短解码操作的资源争夺导致队头阻塞，严重影响交互性能稳定性，而传统聊天机器人服务系统无法有效应对这种混合工作负载。

Method: AgentServe系统采用三项核心技术：(1) 将预填充阶段与解码阶段隔离，避免相互干扰；(2) 对恢复预填充应用动态预算控制；(3) 通过预先建立的CUDA Green Context插槽进行GPU资源分配并实现自适应控制。系统识别代理工作负载的三种类型：处理长系统提示的冷预填充、将工具输出追加到缓存上下文的恢复预填充、以及对延迟敏感的短解码。

Result: 实验评估表明，AgentServe在各种设置下相比最先进的基线系统实现了最高2.8倍的TTFT（首令牌时间）改进和2.7倍的TPOT（每令牌输出时间）改进，同时保持了具有竞争力的吞吐量水平，显著提升了延迟稳定性。

Conclusion: AgentServe成功解决了单GPU上多AI代理执行中的资源竞争和性能不稳定问题，证明了通过阶段隔离、动态预算和CUDA Green Context的自适应资源分配可以有效平衡延迟稳定性和吞吐量，为本地消费级GPU上的AI代理服务提供了有效的解决方案。

Abstract: Large language models (LLMs) are increasingly deployed as AI agents that operate in short reasoning-action loops, interleaving model computation with external calls. Unlike traditional chat applications, these agentic workloads require inference serving systems to balance low latency, stable token emission, and throughput under multiple request arrivals from different AI agents. Recent deployments highlight a shift toward running small language models (SLMs) locally on consumer-grade GPUs, driven by privacy, compliance, and cost constraints. When heterogeneous requests overlap on a single GPU, long prefills and short decodes contend for resources, creating head-of-line blocking that destabilizes interactive performance. By analyzing agent workloads, we observe that their execution naturally separates into cold prefills, which process long system prompts, resume prefills, which append tool outputs to cached contexts, and short decodes, which are latency-critical. This mix intensifies contention compared to conventional chatbot serving. We present AgentServe, a single-GPU serving system that ensures stable multi-agent execution under such conditions by isolating prefills from decodes, applying dynamic budgeting to resume prefills, and allocating GPU resources through pre-established CUDA Green Context slots with adaptive control. Evaluation results show that AgentServe significantly improves latency stability while sustaining competitive throughput, achieving up to 2.8x TTFT improvement and 2.7x TPOT improvement over state-of-the-art baselines across different settings.

</details>


### [135] [S-HPLB: Efficient LLM Attention Serving via Sparsity-Aware Head Parallelism Load Balance](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.10353)
*Di Liu,Yifei Liu,Chen Chen,Zhibin Yu,Xiaoyi Fan,Quan Chen,Minyi Guo*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大语言模型规模和上下文长度增加导致注意力计算成为服务瓶颈。现有方法在多头并行GPU部署时，采用统一稀疏预算忽略了注意力头之间异构但稳定的稀疏弹性特性，且异构稀疏度会导致跨GPU资源气泡问题。

Method: 提出稀疏感知头并行负载均衡（S-HPLB）策略：1）根据注意力头的异构稀疏弹性特性分配头自适应稀疏预算；2）通过负载均衡调度最小化跨GPU资源气泡，优化异构稀疏度下的注意力计算时间一致性。

Result: 在长上下文基准测试上，S-HPLB实现了平均注意力计算延迟2.88倍提升，且无质量下降。

Conclusion: 通过利用注意力头异构稀疏弹性并设计负载均衡部署策略，可有效提升LLM服务效率，为大规模模型推理优化提供了新思路。

Abstract: With the increasing volumes of Large Language Models (LLMs) and the expanding context lengths, attention computation has become a key performance bottleneck in LLM serving. For fast attention computation, recent practices often parallelize the attention heads on multiple GPUs, and also widely adopt attention sparsification to reduce the computation amount -- which selectively computes a subset of attention pairs under a preset sparsity budget. In this paper, we notice that attention heads of an LLM model often exhibit heterogeneous-yet-stable sparsity elasticities, which motivates us to enforce head-adaptive sparsity budgets to attain better efficiency while preserving high inference quality. Yet, from the system aspect, with heterogeneous sparsity levels, attention computation time on different heads would be inconsistent, yielding cross-GPU resource bubbles under head-parallel deployment. To further minimize such bubbles, we propose a novel attention deployment strategy called Sparsity-aware Head-Parallel Load Balance (S-HPLB). Experiments on long-context benchmark show that, S-HPLB can achieve a $2.88\times$ improvement in average attention computation latency without quality degradation.

### [136] [CD-Raft: Reducing the Latency of Distributed Consensus in Cross-Domain Sites](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.10555)
*Yangyang Wang,Ziqian Cheng,Yucong Dong,Zichen Xu*

TL;DR: 本文提出了CD-Raft协议，通过优化跨域站点的RTT和领导节点位置，显著降低了共识延迟，实验证明平均延迟降低32.90%，尾部延迟降低49.24%。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现代大规模AI计算负载导致跨站点（数据中心节点）间的数据同步频繁，共识延迟成为性能瓶颈，尤其在跨域场景下问题更为突出。

Method: 提出CD-Raft协议，通过优化跨域往返时间（RTT）的读写操作以及精心选择领导节点位置来降低共识延迟；使用TLA+形式化规范验证了协议正确性，保证了强一致性；基于YCSB基准进行了原型实现和评估。

Result: 实验结果表明，与经典Raft协议相比，CD-Raft在跨多个站点的知名工作负载下，平均延迟降低32.90%，99分位尾部延迟降低49.24%。

Conclusion: CD-Raft成功解决了跨域站点的共识延迟挑战，在保证强一致性的同时显著提升了系统性能，为跨域分布式系统提供了高效的共识解决方案。

Abstract: Today's massive AI computation loads push heavy data synchronization across sites, i.e., nodes in data centers. Any reduction in such consensus latency can significantly improve the overall performance of desired systems. This consensus challenge explosively peaks at cross-domain sites. In this paper, we proposed CD-Raft to address the cross-domain latency challenge, an optimized Raft protocol for strong consistency in cross-domain sites. CD-Raft can significantly reduce consensus latency by optimizing cross-domain round-trip time (RTT) for reads and writes, as well as carefully positioning the leader node. We verified the correctness of CD-Raft in a formal specification using the TLA+ specification, guaranteeing the strong consistency across sites. We have prototyped CD-Raft and evaluated it using the YCSB benchmark. Empirical results show that compared to the classic Raft, CD-Raft reduces the average latency by 32.90% and (99th percentile) tail latency by 49.24% for renown traces across multiple sites.

### [137] [Double-Precision Matrix Multiplication Emulation via Ozaki-II Scheme with FP8 Quantization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.10634)
*Yuki Uchino,Katsuhisa Ozaki,Toshiyuki Imamura*

Main category: cs.DC

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于FP8矩阵乘累加单元实现双精度矩阵乘法（DGEMM）仿真的新方法，通过改进Ozaki-II方案克服了其无法直接应用于FP8单元的限制，相比Ozaki-I方案显著减少了所需的FP8矩阵乘法次数，适用于新兴GPU架构的高性能计算场景。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在高性能计算（HPC）应用中，FP64算术对确保数值精度和稳定性至关重要，但近年来硬件对FP64性能的提升相对有限。为获得持续的性能增益，需要有效利用高吞吐量的低精度算术（如INT8和FP8）。然而，在NVIDIA Blackwell Ultra和Rubin等新架构中，INT8性能显著降低，仅依赖INT8已不足够，FP8算术的使用变得愈发重要。Ozaki-I和Ozaki-II方案是利用低精度算术仿真DGEMM的基础方法，但Ozaki-II方案的原始算法无法直接适配FP8 MMA单元，存在技术限制。

Method: 本文提出了一种创新技术，使基于Ozaki-II方案的DGEMM仿真能够在FP8矩阵乘累加（MMA）单元上实现。该方法克服了原始Ozaki-II算法无法直接利用FP8 MMA单元的局限，通过算法改进实现了FP64矩阵乘法仿真。与基于相同算法结构的INT8、FP8和FP16 MMA单元的Ozaki-I方案实现不同，本方法专门针对FP8单元优化了Ozaki-II方案的执行方式。

Result: 所提出的方法成功实现了基于FP8 MMA单元的FP64矩阵乘法仿真，解决了Ozaki-II方案无法直接应用于FP8单元的技术难题。与基于FP8的Ozaki-I方案仿真相比，新方法显著减少了所需的FP8矩阵乘法次数，实现了在新兴GPU架构上的高效FP64仿真。

Conclusion: 本研究填补了Ozaki-II方案在FP8 MMA单元应用方面的空白，为在INT8性能受限的新一代GPU架构上实现高效的FP64矩阵乘法仿真提供了可行方案。该方法对于在高性能计算中有效利用FP8高吞吐量算术资源具有重要意义，为未来HPC应用的性能优化提供了新的技术路径。

Abstract: In high-performance computing (HPC) applications, FP64 arithmetic remains indispensable for ensuring numerical accuracy and stability. However, in recent hardware generations, improvements in FP64 arithmetic performance have been relatively modest. Consequently, achieving sustained performance gains for FP64 computations necessitates the effective utilization of high-throughput low-precision arithmetic, such as INT8 and FP8. In several recent architectures, such as NVIDIA Blackwell Ultra and NVIDIA Rubin, INT8 performance has been significantly reduced, making reliance on INT8 alone insufficient. The use of FP8 arithmetic is thus increasingly important. In this paper, we propose a method for emulating double-precision (FP64) general matrix--matrix multiplication (DGEMM), a fundamental and performance-critical kernel in many HPC applications, using FP8 matrix multiply-accumulate (MMA) units. The Ozaki-I and Ozaki-II schemes are well established as foundational approaches for emulating DGEMM via low-precision arithmetic. For DGEMM emulation via the Ozaki-I scheme, implementations using INT8, FP8, and FP16 MMA units have been proposed, all of which can be realized based on the same underlying algorithmic structure. In contrast, although implementations of DGEMM emulation via the Ozaki-II scheme using INT8 MMA units have been reported, the original algorithm cannot be directly adapted to exploit FP8 MMA units. In this work, we introduce a novel technique to overcome this limitation and demonstrate FP64 matrix multiplication emulation based on the Ozaki-II scheme that operates on FP8 MMA units. Compared to FP8-based emulation via the Ozaki-I scheme, our method significantly reduces the number of required FP8 matrix multiplications and enables efficient FP64 emulation on emerging GPU architectures.

</details>


### [138] [Aceso: Carbon-Aware and Cost-Effective Microservice Placement for Small and Medium-sized Enterprises](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.10768)
*Georgia Christofidi,Francisco Álvarez-Terribas,Ioannis Roumpos,Nicolas Kourtellis,Jesus Omaña Iglesias,Thaleia Dimitra Doudali*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 微服务架构在云计算中占据主导地位，但部署复杂。数据中心碳排放量显著，碳感知调度成为缓解策略。然而，现有方案主要针对批处理、高性能计算或无服务器工作负载，且假设拥有全球规模基础设施，这与现实中大多数受限于国家或区域范围的中小企业的实际情况不符。

Method: 提出Aseo系统，一种自适应碳感知与效率感知的微服务放置方案。该方法考虑碳排放、成本和延迟约束，利用基于洞察的搜索空间剪枝技术，通过可扩展的优化策略在地理受限区域内动态放置微服务。

Result: 在真实部署环境中评估显示，Aseo能够快速适应工作负载和碳强度的实时变化。与单一国家内的静态部署相比，平均降低碳排放37.4%，减少运营成本3.6%，同时持续满足服务等级目标（SLOs）。

Conclusion: Aseo成功实现了面向中小企业的、在区域受限基础设施中延迟敏感应用的碳感知与成本感知微服务部署，填补了现有碳感知调度方案在实际中小企业场景中的应用空白。

Abstract: Microservices are a dominant architecture in cloud computing, offering scalability and modularity, but also posing complex deployment challenges. As data centers contribute significantly to global carbon emissions, carbon-aware scheduling has emerged as a promising mitigation strategy. However, most existing solutions target batch, high-performance, or serverless workloads and assume access to global-scale infrastructure. Such an assumption does not hold for many national or regional small to medium-sized enterprises (SMEs) with microservice applications, which represent the real-world majority. In this paper, we present Aceso, an Adaptive Carbon- and Efficiency-aware placement for microservices that considers carbon, cost, and latency constraints. Aceso dynamically places microservices across geographically constrained regions using a scalable optimization strategy that leverages insight-based search space pruning techniques. Evaluation on a real-world deployment shows that Aceso quickly adapts to real-time changes in workload and carbon intensity and reduces carbon emissions by 37.4% and operational cost by 3.6%, on average, compared to a static deployment within a single country, while consistently meeting SLOs. In this way, Aceso enables carbon- and cost-aware microservice deployment for latency-sensitive applications in regionally limited infrastructures for SMEs.

</details>


### [139] [Topological Analysis for Identifying Anomalies in Serverless Platforms](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.10850)
*Gianluca Reali,Mauro Femminella*

Main category: cs.DC

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于拓扑模型和Hodge分解的无服务器平台信息流分析方法，将流量分解为局部可修正分量和全局谐波模式，揭示了谐波流是系统固有结构属性而非配置错误，并提出了包含"阻尼效应"的迭代修复策略来管理流量复杂性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 无服务器平台中的信息流具有复杂性和非保守性特征，这是由于独立部署的函数在平台粗粒度控制机制下的交互方式所导致的。现有的管理方法无法有效应对这种复杂性，需要新的理论框架来理解和处理这些复杂的流量模式。

Method: 提出了一个无服务器服务的拓扑模型，并运用Hodge分解技术将观测到的操作流量分离为两个不同的类别：可以局部修正的分量以及在任意尺度上持续存在的谐波模式。在此基础上，开发了一种迭代方法来分析函数间的流量交互。

Result: 研究发现谐波流自然地从不同类型的函数间交互中产生，应当被理解为无服务器系统的结构属性而非配置错误。实验结果证实，所提出的方法能够揭示潜在的架构结构，并通过引入"阻尼效应"可以有效遏制谐波低效问题，提供了除完全重构服务拓扑模型之外的替代方案。

Conclusion: 本研究为无服务器平台的流量管理提供了新的理论视角和实践工具，证明了拓扑分析和Hodge分解在理解系统结构特性方面的有效性，为实际运营中的问题修复提供了可行的策略指导。

Abstract: The information flows in serverless platforms are complex and non-conservative. This is a direct result of how independently deployed functions interact under the platform coarse-grained control mechanisms. To manage this complexity, we introduce a topological model for serverless services. Using Hodge decomposition, we can separate observed operational flows into two distinct categories. They include components that can be corrected locally and harmonic modes that persist at any scale. Our analysis reveals that these harmonic flows emerge naturally from different types of inter-function interactions. They should be understood as structural properties of serverless systems, not as configuration errors. Building on this insight, we present an iterative method for analyzing inter-function flows. This method helps deriving practical remediation strategies. One such strategy is the introduction of "dumping effects" to contain harmonic inefficiencies, offering an alternative to completely restructuring the service's topological model. Our experimental results confirm that this approach can uncover latent architectural structures.

</details>

### [141] [Tureis: Transformer-based Unified Resilience for IoT Devices in Smart Homes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.10038)
*Alireza Borhani,Vafa Andalibi,Bahar Asgari*

Main category: cs.NI

TL;DR: 本文提出了Tureis，一种面向智能家居IoT系统的自监督、上下文感知的故障检测与故障传感器定位方法，适用于多故障、多居民的边缘部署场景。通过轻量级BERT风格Transformer进行传感器级别的掩码重建，显著提升了故障定位精度，同时保持低计算开销。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 智能家居IoT系统依赖异构传感器网络，但这些低成本、资源受限的传感器在真实环境下极易发生故障。现有方法存在多项局限：假设单一故障和单一居民场景、仅提供故障检测而无法定位具体传感器、覆盖的故障类型和传感器模态有限、需要标签和人工干预，或引入的开销阻碍边缘部署。这些限制阻碍了可靠、精细的故障定位。

Method: Tureis将异构的二值和数值传感器流编码为紧凑的比特级特征，训练一个轻量级BERT风格Transformer，在短时间窗口上进行传感器级别的掩码重建，捕获空间和短期时间相关性。该自监督目标无需标签或语义标注。运行时，Tureis将重建残差转化为传感器级别的故障证据，并采用迭代隔离-继续循环，屏蔽已标记的故障传感器，使其他故障得以显现，实现细粒度定位。

Result: 在包含多达9位居民的五个数据集上，Tureis在单故障定位F1分数上分别比三个强基线提升+7.6%、+21.0%和+25.0%。在多达5个故障传感器的多故障场景中，相比两个基线分别提升+17.6%和+35.4%（第三个基线不适用于此场景）。模型小于1MB，在Raspberry Pi 5上每分钟数据处理仅需几毫秒，峰值内存约0.5GB。

Conclusion: Tureis成功解决了智能家居IoT系统中的多故障、多居民场景下的故障检测与定位问题，在显著提升定位精度的同时保持了边缘设备友好的计算开销，为智能家居系统的可靠性提供了实用解决方案。

Abstract: Smart-home IoT systems rely on heterogeneous sensor networks whose correctness shapes application behavior and the physical environment. However, these low-cost, resource-constrained sensors are highly prone to failure under real-world stressors. Prior methods often assume single-failure, single-resident settings, offer only failure detection rather than sensor-level localization, cover limited fault types and sensor modalities, require labels and human intervention, or impose overheads hindering edge deployment. To overcome these limitations, we propose Tureis, a self-supervised, context-aware method for failure detection and faulty-sensor localization in smart homes, designed for multi-failure, multi-resident edge settings. Tureis encodes heterogeneous binary and numeric sensor streams into compact bit-level features. It then trains a lightweight BERT-style Transformer with sensor-wise masked reconstruction over short-horizon windows, capturing spatial and short-term temporal correlations without mixing unrelated events. This self-supervised objective removes the need for labels or curated semantics. Then, at run-time, Tureis converts reconstruction residuals into sensor-level failure evidence and uses an iterative isolate-and-continue loop that masks flagged sensors, allowing other failures to surface and enabling resilient, fine-grained localization. Across five datasets with up to nine residents, Tureis improves single-failure localization F1 by +7.6%, +21.0%, and +25.0% over three strong baselines. In multi-failure scenarios with up to five faulty sensors, it further boosts localization F1 by +17.6% and +35.4% over two baselines, while the third does not extend to this setting. These gains come with minute-scale localization and an edge-friendly footprint, as a sub-megabyte model that processes each minute of data in a few milliseconds with ~0.5 GB peak memory on a Raspberry Pi 5.

</details>


### [142] [Where Do Flow Semantics Reside? A Protocol-Native Tabular Pretraining Paradigm for Encrypted Traffic Classification](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.10051)
*Sizhe Huang,Shujie Yang*

Main category: cs.NI

TL;DR: 本文揭示了现有自监督掩码建模方法在加密流量分类中因归纳偏置不匹配而失效的根本原因，提出协议原生范式及FlowSem-MAE模型，通过可预测性引导过滤、FSU特定嵌入和双轴注意力机制，在半标注数据下显著超越现有方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有自监督掩码建模方法在加密流量分类中表现不佳：在冻结编码器评估下，准确率从0.9骤降至0.47，未能有效减少对标注数据的依赖。作者认为根本原因在于归纳偏置不匹配：将流量展平为字节序列破坏了协议定义的语义。具体表现为三个问题：（1）字段不可预测性：如ip.id等随机字段无法学习却被作为重建目标；（2）嵌入混淆：语义不同的字段坍缩到统一嵌入空间；（3）元数据丢失：捕获时间元数据被丢弃，影响时序分析。

Method: 提出协议原生范式，将协议定义的字段语义作为架构先验，将任务重新表述为与数据内在表格模态对齐。具体实现为FlowSem-MAE——基于流语义单元（FSU）的表格掩码自编码器，包含三大创新：（1）可预测性引导过滤：聚焦可学习的FSU；（2）FSU特定嵌入：保持字段边界，避免语义混淆；（3）双轴注意力：同时捕获包内和时序模式。

Result: FlowSem-MAE在多个数据集上显著超越现有最先进方法。在仅使用一半标注数据的情况下，性能优于大多数在完整数据上训练的现有方法。

Conclusion: 通过将协议定义的字段语义纳入架构设计，FlowSem-MAE成功解决了现有方法因归纳偏置不匹配导致的性能骤降问题，证明了协议原生范式在加密流量分类中的有效性，为减少对标注数据的依赖提供了新思路。

Abstract: Self-supervised masked modeling shows promise for encrypted traffic classification by masking and reconstructing raw bytes. Yet recent work reveals these methods fail to reduce reliance on labeled data despite costly pretraining: under frozen encoder evaluation, accuracy drops from greater than 0.9 to less than 0.47. We argue the root cause is inductive bias mismatch: flattening traffic into byte sequences destroys protocol-defined semantics. We identify three specific issues: 1) field unpredictability, random fields like ip.id are unlearnable yet treated as reconstruction targets; 2) embedding confusion, semantically distinct fields collapse into a unified embedding space; 3) metadata loss, capture-time metadata essential for temporal analysis is discarded. To address this, we propose a protocol-native paradigm that treats protocol-defined field semantics as architectural priors, reformulating the task to align with the data's intrinsic tabular modality rather than incrementally adapting sequence-based architectures. Instantiating this paradigm, we introduce FlowSem-MAE, a tabular masked autoencoder built on Flow Semantic Units (FSUs). It features predictability-guided filtering that focuses on learnable FSUs, FSU-specific embeddings to preserve field boundaries, and dual-axis attention to capture intra-packet and temporal patterns. FlowSem-MAE significantly outperforms state-of-the-art across datasets. With only half labeled data, it outperforms most existing methods trained on full data.

</details>


### [143] [Performance Evaluation of Delay Tolerant Network Protocols to Improve Nepal Earthquake Rescue Communications](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.10153)
*Xiaofei Liu,Milena Radenkovic*

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在灾害救援和极端环境通信领域，延迟容忍网络（DTN）因其"存储-携带-转发"机制成为重要技术。选择合适的路由策略对于提高求救消息传输成功率和减少物资调度延迟至关重要。

Method: 基于尼泊尔加德满都地震救援的动态人口分布模型和初期救援活动特征设计伪真实用例；识别多个现实节点组（受灾居民、救援队、无人机和地面车辆），根据各组移动行为建立通信模型；在不同救援队节点缓冲区大小下，对两种基准路由协议进行多准则性能分析，评估投递概率、平均延迟、跳数和缓冲时间等指标。

Result: 验证了分布式DTN通信方法在尼泊尔地震救援用例中的有效性；揭示了不同路由协议在灾害通信环境中传输可靠性与资源利用之间存在权衡关系；为基于边缘节点的下一代应急通信服务设计提供了依据。

Conclusion: 研究证明了DTN技术在灾害救援场景中的实用价值，通过多层级复杂数据和协议差异分析，为设计下一代基于边缘节点的应急通信服务提供了理论基础和实践参考。

Abstract: In the fields of disaster rescue and communication in extreme environments, Delay Tolerant Network (DTN) has become an important technology due to its "store-carry-forward" mechanism. Selecting the appropriate routing strategy is of crucial significance for improving the success rate of distress message transmission and reducing delays in material dispatch. We design a pseudo realistic use case of Nepal Kathmandu earthquake rescue based on dynamically changing population distribution model and characteristics of rescue activities in the initial rescue efforts in Nepal Kathmandu earthquakes to conducted the multi criteria two benchmark routing protocols performance analysis in the face of different buffer sizes of the rescue team nodes. We identify multiple real world node groups, including affected residents, rescue teams, drones and ground vehicles and communication models are established according to the movement behaviors of these groups. We analyze the communication of distress messages between edge nodes to obtain performance metrics such as delivered probability, average delay, hop count, and buffer time. By analyzing the multi layer complex data and protocols differences, the research results show the effectiveness of distributed DTN communication methods in the Nepal earthquake rescue use case, reveal existence of trade-offs between transmission reliability and resource utilization of different routing protocols in disaster communication environment and provide a basis for the design of next-generation emergency communication services based on edge nodes.

### [144] [Utility Function is All You Need: LLM-based Congestion Control](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.10357)
*Neta Rozen-Schiff,Liron Schiff,Stefan Schmid*

Main category: cs.NI

TL;DR: 本文提出GenCC框架，利用大语言模型（LLM）自动生成拥塞控制效用函数，相比现有最优协议性能提升37%-142%。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 拥塞控制是通信网络中的关键问题。在分布式环境中，应用程序无法直接协作，需要通过效用函数优化发送速率。然而，当不同应用有不同优化目标时，手工设计效用函数变得极其复杂，需要大量数学分析和实验验证。

Method: 提出GenCC框架，将大语言模型的代码生成能力与真实网络测试平台相结合，自动设计拥塞控制效用函数。该框架探索了两种指导策略：生成式代码进化策略和数学思维链（Chain-of-Thought），以生成满足特定应用需求的协议。

Result: 实验结果表明，通过生成式代码进化策略或数学思维链指导的LLM能够生成接近最优的拥塞控制协议，相比现有最先进的拥塞控制协议，性能提升37%-142%。

Conclusion: LLM结合适当的指导策略可以有效解决拥塞控制效用函数设计这一复杂优化问题，为网络协议设计提供了新的自动化方法。

Abstract: Congestion is a critical and challenging problem in communication networks. Congestion control protocols allow network applications to tune their sending rate in a way that optimizes their performance and the network utilization. In the common distributed setting, the applications cannot collaborate with each other directly but instead obtain similar estimations about the state of the network using latency and loss measurements. These measurements can be fed into analytical functions, referred to by utility functions, whose gradients help each and all distributed senders to converge to a desired state.
  The above process becomes extremely complicated when each application has different optimization goals and requirements. Crafting these utilization functions has been a research subject for over a decade, with small incremental changes requiring rigorous mathematical analysis as well as real-world experiments.
  In this work, we present GenCC, a framework leveraging the code generation capabilities of large language models (LLMs) coupled with realistic network testbed, to design congestion control utility functions. Using GenCC, we analyze the impact of different guidance strategies on the performance of the generated protocols, considering application-specific requirements and network capacity.
  Our results show that LLMs, guided by either a generative code evolution strategy or mathematical chain-of-thought (CoT), can obtain close to optimal results, improving state-of-the-art congestion control protocols by 37%-142%, depending on the scenario.

</details>


### [145] [A Secure Splitting and Acceleration Strategy for TCP/QUIC in Interplanetary Networks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.10437)
*Jianhao Yu,Ye Li,Qingfang Jiang,Shuai Liu,Wenfeng Li,Kanglian Zhao*

Main category: cs.NI

TL;DR: 本文针对星际网络中高时延、高丢包和频繁中断导致传统传输协议性能严重退化的问题，提出了一种基于非透明安全代理架构的安全传输加速策略，并通过PEPspace原型系统在典型地月场景中验证了其有效性和优越性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 星际网络具有极高时延、高丢包率和频繁中断等独特特征，导致传统传输协议（TCP和QUIC）性能严重退化，亟需设计专门针对IPN环境的传输加速方案来保障数据传输的高效性和可靠性。

Method: 提出非透明安全代理（NTSP）架构实现端到端加密流的连接分割同时保持应用层安全；基于NTSP设计IPN感知传输策略，包括：(i)利用深空链路预调度特性的基于速率的拥塞控制算法；(ii)无需重传的自适应分组级前向纠错方案；(iii)理论驱动的背压流控机制及最优缓冲区建模。通过PEPspace原型系统实现并在地月场景中进行评估。

Result: 在地月场景评估中，该策略实现了接近容量的稳定吞吐量，相比TCP/QUIC变体及现有性能增强代理显著提升了传输性能，同时在间歇性链路中保持低时延和鲁棒的数据交付能力。

Conclusion: 所提出的NTSP架构和安全传输加速策略有效解决了IPN环境中的传输性能瓶颈，为未来统一IP/DTN架构提供了基础框架，弥合了异构空间网络中的关键架构差距。

Abstract: Interplanetary networks (IPNs) present unique challenges such as extreme delay, high loss, and frequent disruptions that severely degrade the performance of conventional transport protocols like Transmission Control Protocol (TCP) and Quick UDP Internet Connection (QUIC). To address these issues, we propose a secure transport acceleration strategy tailored for IPNs. This strategy is founded on our Non-Transparent Secure Proxy (NTSP) architecture, which enables connection splitting for end-to-end encrypted flows while preserving application layer security. Based on the NTSP, we design an IPN-aware transport policy that combines (i) a rate-based congestion control algorithm exploiting the pre-scheduled nature of deep-space links to achieve stable and efficient bandwidth utilization, and (ii) an adaptive packet-level forward error correction scheme to provide low-latency loss recovery without retransmissions. Furthermore, we introduce a theoretically grounded backpressure flow control mechanism, deriving an analytical model for optimal buffer sizing to mitigate rate mismatch and prevent bufferbloat. The strategy is implemented in a prototype system, PEPspace, and evaluated in representative Earth-Moon scenarios. Results show near-capacity and stable goodput and substantially improved delivery performance compared with TCP/QUIC variants and existing Performance Enhancing Proxies, while maintaining low latency and robust data delivery across intermittent links. The NTSP architecture is further discussed as a foundational framework for future unified IP/DTN architectures, bridging a key architectural gap in heterogeneous space networks.

</details>


### [146] [Q-StaR: A Quasi-Static Routing Scheme for NoCs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.10637)
*Yang Zhang,Yiren Zhao,Xu Wang,Fengyuan Ren*

Main category: cs.NI

TL;DR: Q-StaR是一种片上网络路由方案，通过N-Rank提取拓扑和流量分布决定的长期负载趋势，指导BiDOR的运行时路由选择，在保持静态路由简单性和可预测性的同时显著提升负载均衡性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 片上网络中，静态路由方案虽然具有简单性和可预测性优势，但由于无法感知运行时负载分布，难以有效平衡网络负载。

Method: Q-StaR发现拓扑和流量分布是决定负载分布长期趋势的两个关键因素，提出N-Rank方法提取该趋势，并利用所得信息指导BiDOR在运行时进行路由选择。

Result: 仿真实验表明，Q-StaR显著优于典型的维序路由：均匀流量下吞吐量提升42.9%，真实工作负载下平均延迟降低86.4%，最大延迟降低95.3%。

Conclusion: Q-StaR成功在保留静态路由简单性和可预测性的前提下，通过利用负载分布的长期趋势信息实现了显著的负载均衡性能提升。

Abstract: In networks-on-chip, static routing schemes are favored for their simplicity and predictability, but they cannot effectively balance network load due to the unawareness of runtime load distribution. Q-StaR discovers two factors (topology and traffic distribution) that determine the long-term trend of load distribution, and proposes N-Rank to extract this trend. The obtained information is used to guide BiDOR's route selection at runtime, thereby improving load balancing while retaining simplicity and predictability. Simulation validates that Q-StaR significantly outperforms the typical dimension-order routing (throughput under uniform traffic improved by 42.9\%, and mean/maximum latency under realistic workloads reduced by 86.4\%/95.3\%).

</details>


### [147] [Towards Intelligent Spectrum Management: Spectrum Demand Estimation Using Graph Neural Networks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.10802)
*Mohamad Alkadamani,Amir Ghasemi,Halim Yanikomeroglu*

Main category: cs.NI

TL;DR: 本文提出了HR-GAT模型，通过图注意力网络在多层次多分辨率框架下对频谱需求进行精细空间尺度估算，在五个加拿大城市的测试中相比最佳基线方法降低了约21%的中位RMSE，为频谱共享和分配提供了监管者可访问的需求地图。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 无线连接需求的不断增长与有限的频谱资源之间的矛盾迫切需要更高效的频谱管理。频谱共享是一种有前景的方法，但监管机构需要准确的方法来刻画需求动态并指导分配决策。

Method: 基于公共部署记录构建并验证频谱需求代理指标，采用图注意力网络（GAT）构建层次化、多分辨率框架（HR-GAT）模型。该模型能够捕捉邻域效应和跨尺度模式，减少空间自相关并提升泛化能力。

Result: 在五个加拿大城市进行评估，并与八个竞争性基线方法对比。HR-GAT相比最佳替代方案将中位RMSE降低约21%，同时降低了残差空间偏差。生成的需求地图对监管者易于访问。

Conclusion: HR-GAT模型能够有效估计精细空间尺度的频谱需求，为频谱共享和无线网络中的频谱分配决策提供支持，有助于监管机构进行更精准的频谱管理和资源分配。

Abstract: The growing demand for wireless connectivity, combined with limited spectrum resources, calls for more efficient spectrum management. Spectrum sharing is a promising approach; however, regulators need accurate methods to characterize demand dynamics and guide allocation decisions. This paper builds and validates a spectrum demand proxy from public deployment records and uses a graph attention network in a hierarchical, multi-resolution setup (HR-GAT) to estimate spectrum demand at fine spatial scales. The model captures both neighborhood effects and cross-scale patterns, reducing spatial autocorrelation and improving generalization. Evaluated across five Canadian cities and against eight competitive baselines, HR-GAT reduces median RMSE by roughly 21% relative to the best alternative and lowers residual spatial bias. The resulting demand maps are regulator-accessible and support spectrum sharing and spectrum allocation in wireless networks.

</details>


### [148] [Expressive Boundedness of Authoritative DNS Response Selection](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.10897)
*Chris Bertinato*

Main category: cs.NI

TL;DR: 本文形式化定义了权威DNS响应选择机制，证明了其语义受DNS协议约束而具有有界性，建立了统一的代数框架用于跨异构DNS系统的等价性、可表示性和近似性分析。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前权威DNS响应选择（如流量引导）在实践中广泛部署，但其语义缺乏独立于特定配置语言或实现的形式化定义，导致难以进行跨系统的精确推理和分析。

Method: 基于DNS协议约束（响应有限性、RRset原子性、终止性、可缓存性、解析器可见输入限制），将权威响应选择形式化为一类DNS可容许函数，证明其存在有限正规形式（条件约束+有限候选集选择），并揭示其内在的代数结构。

Result: 证明权威DNS响应选择语义域具有有界性，每个可容许函数均存在有限正规形式；该域具有DNS语义诱导的内在代数结构，支持对组合、表达能力损失和语义坍缩的原理性推理；可统一建模具体授权系统、配置模型和序列化编码。

Conclusion: 所提出的框架支持跨异构权威DNS系统进行基于协议语义而非实现细节的等价性、可表示性和近似性精确推理，为DNS系统设计和分析提供了理论基础。

Abstract: Authoritative Domain Name System (DNS) response selection defines query-time response selection based on resolver-visible context and per-answer metadata, yielding different observable outcomes for the same query under different conditions. Although such behavior is widely deployed and often described informally as traffic steering, its semantics have not been formalized independently of particular configuration languages or implementations.
  This paper shows that authoritative DNS response selection inhabits a bounded semantic domain determined directly by DNS protocol constraints. Requirements such as finiteness of responses, RRset atomicity, termination, cacheability, and restriction to resolver-visible inputs jointly limit the expressive power of any query-time selection mechanism. We formalize authoritative response selection as a class of DNS-admissible functions and prove that every such function admits a finite normal form consisting of conditional restriction over observable context followed by selection among a finite candidate set.
  We further show that this bounded semantic domain carries intrinsic algebraic structure induced by DNS semantics, enabling principled reasoning about composition, expressiveness loss, and semantic collapse. Concrete authoritative systems, configuration models, and serialized encodings are modeled uniformly as semantic restrictions of this domain. This framework supports precise reasoning about equivalence, representability, and approximation across heterogeneous authoritative DNS systems, grounded directly in protocol semantics rather than implementation detail.

</details>


### [149] [Measurement-Driven O-RAN Diagnostics with Tail Latency and Scheduler Indicators](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.11023)
*Theofanis P. Raptis,Weronika Maria Bachan,Roberto Verdone*

Main category: cs.NI

TL;DR: 本文通过真实测量活动，对O-RAN实例进行了跨层性能诊断研究。通过分析应用层延迟尾部特性（如95分位数）与无线层行为（如调度、链路自适应指标）的关联，揭示了UE差异、距离与负载对尾延迟的系统性影响，并提出了结合尾延迟与无线指标的轻量级"退化标志"方法，支持O-RAN的实际监测与故障排查。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有文献多聚焦于吞吐量、仿真环境或单层KPI，缺乏基于真实测量的O-RAN跨层诊断方法。作者旨在通过联合分析应用层延迟与无线层行为，揭示端到端延迟看似稳定但无线层动态仍可检测的情况，从而弥补跨层证据缺失的问题。

Method: 在真实O-RAN环境中进行测量实验，涵盖多种链路距离（2、6、11米）、两种UE配置（商用智能手机和基于调制解调器的设备），包括静态条件和受控动态阻塞场景。采用尾聚焦延迟表征（95分位数、超越概率）而非平均值，并将其与调度器和链路自适应指标（误块行为、调制编码选择、信号质量）相关联分析。

Result: 研究发现：(i) UE依赖性差异主要表现在延迟尾部；(ii) 尾延迟随距离和负载系统性增长；(iii) 存在端到端延迟看似稳定但仍可检测到无线层动态的情况，证明了跨层分析的必要性。基于此提出了结合尾延迟与无线指标的轻量级、基于窗口的"退化标志"方法。

Conclusion: 本文贡献了一套基于测量的可解释O-RAN诊断方法论，区别于现有以吞吐量、仿真或单层KPI为中心的研究。提出的轻量级"退化标志"能够结合尾延迟和无线指标，为实际O-RAN监测和故障排查提供有效支持。

Abstract: We investigate cross-layer performance diagnostics for an O-RAN instance by jointly analyzing application-level latency and radio-layer behavior from a real measurement campaign. Measurements were conducted at multiple link distances (2, 6 and 11 meters) using two representative UE configurations (a commercial smartphone and a modem-based device), under both static conditions and a controlled dynamic obstruction scenario. Rather than relying on averages, the study adopts tail-focused latency characterization (e.g., 95th percentile and exceedance probabilities) and connects it to scheduler- and link-adaptation indicators (e.g., block error behavior, modulation/coding selection and signal quality). The results reveal (i) UE-dependent differences that primarily manifest in the latency tail, (ii) systematic scaling of tail latency with distance and payload and (iii) cases where radio-layer dynamics are detectable even when end-to-end latency appears stable, motivating the need for cross-layer evidence. Distinct from much of the existing literature (often centered on throughput, simulated setups, or single-layer KPIs) this work contributes a measurement-driven methodology for interpretable O-RAN diagnostics and proposes lightweight, window-based "degradation flags" that combine tail latency and radio indicators to support practical monitoring and troubleshooting.

</details>
